Features initial import capability using \"Load Graph\" voice command for MindManager, Freemind, and GraphML format files.\r\n\r\nWhy - Loci uses three core concepts to help you organize, understand and remember; mind maps let you break a problem down into component parts to organize and do analysis, mixed reality interaction with mind maps lets you visualize in 3D to understand how they are related, and the method of loci persistent placement of mind map nodes lets you improve your recall of the mind map, even when you are not using the Loci software. Loci uses voice, gaze and gestures to enable you to make your 3D graphs (mind maps).
